### [188] [Clarification of `Algorithmic Collusion without Threats'](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22232)
*Jason Hartline*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过概念分析和逻辑推理，对Arunachaleswaran等人(2025)提出的场景进行重新解释和澄清，区分合谋行为与非对称竞争行为。

Result: 明确指出Arunachaleswaran等人(2025)描述的"无威胁算法合谋"实际上是一个参与者采取非竞争性策略、另一个参与者采取竞争性策略的非对称互动场景，而非真正的合谋。

Abstract: This brief note clarifies that the scenario described in Arunachaleswaran et al. (2025) -- titled `Algorithmic Collusion without Threats' -- is not one of collusion, but one where one player is behaving non-competitively and the other is behaving competitively.

### [189] [How Many Votes is a Lie Worth? Measuring Strategyproofness through Resource Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22838)
*Ratip Emin Berker,Vincent Conitzer,Eden Hartman,Jiayuan Liu,Caspar Oesterheld*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 提出一种量化投票规则操纵潜力的新框架：通过计算需要添加多少份真实投票才能达到与最佳操纵相同的结果来衡量操纵激励，并应用该框架分析常见投票规则的操纵潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gibbard-Satterthwaite定理表明，当候选人多于两个时，任何非独裁投票规则都可能被不诚实的选民操纵。但不同投票规则下的操纵激励强度如何？需要一种原则性的方法来量化和比较不同投票规则的操纵潜力。

Method: 提出新的量化框架：衡量策略性选民的潜在优势时，计算需要添加多少份其真实投票的副本才能达到与其最佳操纵相同的结果。应用该框架分析广泛的社会选择函数类别，包括位置计分规则、多数一致性规则和孔多塞一致性规则。

Result: 1. 位置计分规则中，操纵潜力最小的是Borda计数（当选民数超过候选人数时）或Plurality（反之）；2. 满足弱多数一致性（包括所有孔多塞一致性规则）的规则无法超越Plurality；3. 多数主义孔多塞规则表现显著更差；4. 在分析的规则中，只有Borda计数的操纵潜力不随选民数量增长。

Conclusion: 建立了不同投票规则在操纵潜力方面的清晰分离，为寻找提供最小操纵激励的投票规则铺平了道路。Borda计数在操纵潜力方面表现突出，是唯一不随选民数量增长的规则。

Abstract: It is well known, by the Gibbard-Satterthwaite Theorem, that when there are more than two candidates, any non-dictatorial voting rule can be manipulated by untruthful voters. But how strong is the incentive to manipulate under different voting rules? We suggest measuring the potential advantage of a strategic voter by asking how many copies of their (truthful) vote must be added to the election in order to achieve an outcome as good as their best manipulation. Intuitively, this definition quantifies what a voter can gain by manipulating in comparison to what they would have gained by finding like-minded voters to join the election. The higher the former is, the more incentive a voter will have to manipulate, even when it is computationally costly.
  Using this framework, we obtain a principled method to measure and compare the manipulation potential for different voting rules. We analyze and report this potential for well-known and broad classes of social choice functions. In particular, we show that the positional scoring rule with the smallest manipulation potential will always be either Borda Count (if the number of voters outweighs the number of candidates) or Plurality (vice versa). Further, we prove that any rule satisfying a weak form of majority consistency (and therefore any Condorcet-consistent rule) cannot outperform Plurality, and that any majoritarian Condorcet rule will perform significantly worse. Consequently, out of the voting rules we analyze, Borda Count stands out as the only one with a manipulation potential that does not grow with the number of voters. By establishing a clear separation between different rules in terms of manipulation potential, our work paves the way for the search for rules that provide voters with minimal incentive to manipulate.

</details>


### [190] [Robust Information Design for Multi-Agent Systems with Complementarities: Smallest-Equilibrium Threshold Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22915)
*Farzaneh Farhadi,Maria Chli*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究具有二元行动和策略互补性的多智能体系统中的信息设计，设计者通过信号影响行为，智能体采用诱导贝叶斯博弈的最小均衡，提出阈值规则实现完美协调


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多智能体系统中，当存在策略互补性时，外部设计者只能通过信号影响智能体行为。智能体采用保守的、厌恶协调的最小均衡行为，这反映了分布式系统的典型特征。需要找到一种鲁棒的信息设计方法，确保在各种均衡选择下都能实现最优协调。

Method: 假设效用函数具有凸势函数且社会福利是凸的。提出构造性阈值规则：为每个状态计算一维得分，对状态排序，选择单一阈值（最多一个状态使用临界彩票）。该规则是线性规划最优顶点，满足可行性和顺序服从约束。

Result: 鲁棒可实施的最优解具有简单形式：每个状态下实现完美协调（要么所有智能体行动，要么都不行动）。在疫苗接种和技术采用两个实证领域，构造性策略与线性规划最优解匹配，时间复杂度为O(|Θ|log|Θ|)，避免了仅考虑服从约束的设计所预测的夸大福利。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有互补性的多智能体系统提供了一种通用、可扩展的鲁棒协调方法。阈值规则简单易实现，能够处理智能体的保守均衡选择行为，确保设计者的信号策略在各种均衡实现下都有效。

Abstract: We study information design in multi-agent systems (MAS) with binary actions and strategic complementarities, where an external designer influences behavior only through signals. Agents play the smallest-equilibrium of the induced Bayesian game, reflecting conservative, coordination-averse behavior typical in distributed systems. We show that when utilities admit a convex potential and welfare is convex, the robustly implementable optimum has a remarkably simple form: perfect coordination at each state: either everyone acts or no one does. We provide a constructive threshold rule: compute a one-dimensional score for each state, sort states, and pick a single threshold (with a knife-edge lottery for at most one state). This rule is an explicit optimal vertex of a linear program (LP) characterized by feasibility and sequential obedience constraints. Empirically, in both vaccination and technology-adoption domains, our constructive policy matches LP optima, scales as $O(|Θ|\log|Θ|)$, and avoids the inflated welfare predicted by obedience-only designs that assume the designer can dictate the (best) equilibrium. The result is a general, scalable recipe for robust coordination in MAS with complementarities.

</details>


### [191] [Social Welfare in Budget Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23027)
*Javier Cembrano,Rupert Freeman,Ulrike Schmidt-Kraepelin,Markus Utke*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了ℓ₁效用下的预算聚合问题，提出了新的比例机制UtilProp和GreedyDecomp，分析了比例性、社会福利和真实性之间的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期研究关注社会福利最大化，但这可能导致少数群体代表性不足。现有的比例性概念（单偏好比例性）较弱，只约束极端偏好情况。需要更好地理解比例性及其与社会福利、真实性之间的相互作用。

Method: 1. 引入比例性代价概念，衡量实现比例性所需牺牲的社会福利；2. 提出新的单偏好比例且真实的机制UtilProp；3. 定义实例级社会福利支配关系来比较机制；4. 研究可分解性并提出GreedyDecomp机制；5. 分析计算最优可分解机制UtilDecomp的计算复杂性。

Result: 1. UtilProp实现了最优的最坏情况比例性代价；2. UtilProp在福利上支配所有已知的单偏好比例且真实的机制；3. GreedyDecomp是可分解机制，具有最优的最坏情况福利比；4. 计算UtilDecomp是NP难的，GreedyDecomp为其提供2-近似福利解。

Conclusion: 通过引入新的比例机制和理论分析，证明了可以在不牺牲社会福利保证的情况下实现更强的比例性概念，为集体决策中的公平与效率权衡提供了新的理论框架和实用机制。

Abstract: We study budget aggregation under $\ell_1$-utilities, a model for collective decision making in which agents with heterogeneous preferences must allocate a public budget across a set of alternatives. Each agent reports their preferred allocation, and a mechanism selects an allocation. Early work focused on social welfare maximization, which in this setting admits truthful mechanisms, but may underrepresent minority groups, motivating the study of proportional mechanisms. However, the dominant proportionality notion, single-minded proportionality, is weak, as it only constrains outcomes when agents hold extreme preferences. To better understand proportionality and its interaction with welfare and truthfulness, we address three questions. First, how much welfare must be sacrificed to achieve proportionality? We formalize this via the price of proportionality, the best worst-case welfare ratio between a proportional mechanism and Util, the welfare-maximizing mechanism. We introduce a new single-minded proportional and truthful mechanism, UtilProp, and show that it achieves the optimal worst-case ratio. Second, how do proportional mechanisms compare in terms of welfare? We define an instance-wise welfare dominance relation and use it to compare mechanisms from the literature. In particular, we show that UtilProp welfare-dominates all previously known single-minded proportional and truthful mechanisms. Third, can stronger notions of proportionality be achieved without compromising welfare guarantees? We answer this question in the affirmative by studying decomposability and proposing GreedyDecomp, a decomposable mechanism with optimal worst-case welfare ratio. We further show that computing the welfare-dominant decomposable mechanism, UtilDecomp, is NP-hard, and that GreedyDecomp provides a 2-approximation to UtilDecomp in terms of welfare.

</details>


### [192] [Impacts of Aggregation on Model Diversity and Consumer Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23293)
*Kate Donahue,Manish Raghavan*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究发现传统胜率指标会激励模型同质化，提出加权胜率机制能促进模型专业化，提升消费者福利


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AI工具市场中，用户通过选择最适合特定任务的模型可以获得比单一模型更好的性能。然而，当前基于胜率的评估标准可能导致模型同质化，降低消费者福利，需要设计更好的激励机制

Method: 研究两种模型变化：市场进入（新增模型）和模型替换（改变现有模型特性）。分析传统胜率指标的激励问题，提出加权胜率机制，该机制根据答案质量给予不同权重，并在理论分析和实证数据集上验证

Result: 传统胜率指标会激励模型创建者使模型同质化，降低消费者福利。提出的加权胜率机制能有效激励生产者创建专业化模型，提高消费者福利。理论结果在实证基准数据集上得到验证

Conclusion: 当前LLM评估中广泛使用的胜率基准存在激励问题，会导致模型同质化。加权胜率机制能提供更好的激励，促进模型专业化，提高市场效率。这对评估设计有重要启示

Abstract: Consider a marketplace of AI tools, each with slightly different strengths and weaknesses. By selecting the right model for the task at hand, a user can do better than simply committing to a single model for everything. Routers operate under a similar principle, where sophisticated model selection can increase overall performance. However, aggregation is often noisy, reflecting in imperfect user choices or routing decisions. This leads to two main questions: first, what does a "healthy marketplace" of models look like for maximizing consumer utility? Secondly, how can we incentivize producers to create such models? Here, we study two types of model changes: market entry (where an entirely new model is created and added to the set of available models), and model replacement (where an existing model has its strengths and weaknesses changed). We show that winrate, a standard benchmark in LLM evaluation, can incentivize model creators to homogenize for both types of model changes, reducing consumer welfare. We propose a new mechanism, weighted winrate, which rewards models for answers that are higher quality, and show that it provably improves incentives for producers to specialize and increases consumer welfare. We conclude by demonstrating that our theoretical results generalize to empirical benchmark datasets and discussing implications for evaluation design.

</details>

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [193] [An automatic counting algorithm for the quantification and uncertainty analysis of the number of microglial cells trainable in small and heterogeneous datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22974)
*L. Martino,M. M. Garcia,P. S. Paradas,E. Curbelo*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出一种基于核方法的自动细胞计数算法，用于大鼠腰椎脊髓切片中的小胶质细胞计数，无需细胞检测，直接进行计数任务


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动细胞计数耗时且需要人员培训，传统自动颜色分析方法只能提供标记区域和强度信息，无法准确提供细胞数量。高分辨率图像中包含大量噪声和伪影，需要更精确的计数方法。

Method: 首先进行预处理生成多个过滤图像以提取特征，然后设计非参数非线性核计数器。该方法只需一个超参数，易于在小数据集上训练，同时足够灵活以处理丰富异构数据集。算法还提供预测不确定性估计，并能处理多个专家对同一图像的意见。

Result: 在人工和真实数据集上的数值实验显示出非常有前景的结果，表明该方法在细胞计数任务中表现良好。

Conclusion: 提出的核计数器方法能够有效解决小胶质细胞计数问题，避免了传统方法的局限性，提供了更准确和可靠的细胞计数解决方案，并附带Matlab代码实现。

Abstract: Counting immunopositive cells on biological tissues generally requires either manual annotation or (when available) automatic rough systems, for scanning signal surface and intensity in whole slide imaging. In this work, we tackle the problem of counting microglial cells in lumbar spinal cord cross-sections of rats by omitting cell detection and focusing only on the counting task. Manual cell counting is, however, a time-consuming task and additionally entails extensive personnel training. The classic automatic color-based methods roughly inform about the total labeled area and intensity (protein quantification) but do not specifically provide information on cell number. Since the images to be analyzed have a high resolution but a huge amount of pixels contain just noise or artifacts, we first perform a pre-processing generating several filtered images {(providing a tailored, efficient feature extraction)}. Then, we design an automatic kernel counter that is a non-parametric and non-linear method. The proposed scheme can be easily trained in small datasets since, in its basic version, it relies only on one hyper-parameter. However, being non-parametric and non-linear, the proposed algorithm is flexible enough to express all the information contained in rich and heterogeneous datasets as well (providing the maximum overfit if required). Furthermore, the proposed kernel counter also provides uncertainty estimation of the given prediction, and can directly tackle the case of receiving several expert opinions over the same image. Different numerical experiments with artificial and real datasets show very promising results. Related Matlab code is also provided.

</details>


### [194] [Uncertainty-Aware Calculation of Analytical Gradients of Matrix-Interpolatory Reduced-Order Models for Efficient Structural Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23314)
*Marcel Warzecha,Sebastian Resch-Schopper,Gerhard Müller*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出一种用于参数化动力系统优化的自适应采样算法，结合投影降阶模型、稀疏贝叶斯回归和Thompson采样，通过梯度搜索迭代优化设计参数


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统采样策略追求全局近似误差最小化，计算成本高。本文旨在开发一种能早期识别并细化有前景区域、减少昂贵全阶模型评估的自适应采样框架

Method: 1) 使用迭代有理Krylov算法对采样全阶模型降阶并重投影到全局基；2) 在降阶算子矩阵元素级进行稀疏贝叶斯回归实现参数化；3) 利用多项式系数后验分布进行Thompson采样处理回归模型不确定性；4) 在参数化降阶模型上执行基于伴随灵敏度分析的梯度搜索获取新样本点；5) 迭代地将找到的最优点加入样本集进行细化

Result: 算法在Timoshenko梁和Kelvin单元两个模型上测试，使用传递函数不同范数作为目标函数，1-2个几何参数作为设计变量。结果显示算法能鲁棒收敛到全局最优，但梯度优化引入显著计算成本

Conclusion: 该自适应采样算法能有效优化参数化动力系统，概率扩展无缝集成到现有矩阵插值降阶框架中，支持不确定性下的解析梯度计算。梯度搜索虽增加计算成本，但能实现鲁棒收敛

Abstract: This paper presents an adaptive sampling algorithm tailored for the optimization of parametrized dynamical systems using projection-based model order reduction. Unlike classical sampling strategies, this framework does not aim for a small approximation error in the global sense but focuses on identifying and refining promising regions early on while reducing expensive full order model evaluations. The algorithm is tested on two models: a Timoshenko beam and a Kelvin cell, which ought to be optimized in terms of the system output in the frequency domain. For that, different norms of the transfer function are used as the objective function, while up to two geometrical parameters form the vector of design variables. The sampled full order models are reduced using the iterative rational Krylov algorithm and reprojected into a global basis. Subsequently, the models are parametrized by performing sparse Bayesian regression on matrix entry level of the reduced operators. Thompson sampling is carried out using the posterior distribution of the polynomial coefficients in order to account for uncertainties in the trained regression models. The strategy deployed for sample acquisition incorporates a gradient-based search on the parametrized reduced order model, which involves analytical gradients obtained via adjoint sensitivity analysis. By adding the found optimum to the sample set, the sample set is iteratively refined. Results demonstrate robust convergence towards the global optimum but highlight the computational cost introduced by the gradient-based optimization. The probabilistic extensions seamlessly integrate into existing matrix-interpolatory reduction frameworks and enable the analytical calculation of gradients under uncertainty.

</details>
